[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mcom.example.SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput[0m[1m([0mSimpleLoggerFuzzer.jav[1;92ma:42[0m[1m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         DEDUP_TOKEN: 03a39a742f79fa3d                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         == libFuzzer crashing input ==                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mReport[0m===                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         # Evaluation Report                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Summary                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         A Jazzer fuzzing run triggered a critical security alert for a remote JNDI lookup   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         in the Log4j library. The fuzzer input caused Log4j’s `JndiLookup` mechanism to     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attempt a lookup on an attacker-controlled remote URL. Depending on the Java        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         runtime version, this behavior can enable remote code execution or unauthorized     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         data exfiltration.                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - What the issue is                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           During pattern-based message formatting in Log4j, an attacker-controlled string   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         was interpreted as a JNDI lookup expression. This led to an actual remote JNDI      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         lookup being performed. The Jazzer sanitizer [1m([0m`NamingContextLookup.lookupHook`[1m)[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         intercepted the call and reported it as a `FuzzerSecurityIssueCritical: Remote JNDI [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Lookup`.                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Vulnerability type                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           Remote JNDI lookup vulnerability, which may permit:                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Remote code execution [1m([0mRCE[1m)[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • Exfiltration of sensitive information via the retrieved naming context          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Important observations and findings                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The crash report shows the sanitizer detecting a remote JNDI lookup at          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `NamingContextLookup.lookupHook` [1m([0mJazzer sanitizer[1m)[0m.                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The lookup originates in                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup.lookup`, invoked during pattern    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         substitution by `StrSubstitutor` and `PatternLayout`.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The fuzzer harness [1m([0m`SimpleLoggerFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[1m)[0m feeds              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         attacker-controlled input directly into the Log4j logging pipeline, triggering the  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         lookup.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           • The issue was flagged before any actual network call or payload delivery,       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         indicating the vulnerability can be discovered purely by input-driven pattern       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         resolution.                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - Codebase areas to investigate                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m1[0m. **JndiLookup logic** [1m([0m`org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup`[1m)[0m – how [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         it parses and performs lookups, especially handling of remote URLs.                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m2[0m. **Pattern resolution components** [1m([0m`StrSubstitutor`, `Interpolator`,           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `MessagePatternConverter`, `PatternLayout`[1m)[0m – the chain that expands `$[1m{[0mjndi:…[1m}[0m`    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         tokens.                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m3[0m. **Sanitizer hook**                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m([0m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.NamingContextLookup`[1m)[0m – how and when JNDI [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         calls are intercepted and reported.                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m4[0m. **Fuzzer harness** [1m([0m`SimpleLoggerFuzzer`[1m)[0m – although not the root cause, it    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         demonstrates how untrusted input flows into the logging subsystem.                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           [1;36m5[0m. **Configuration settings** – any Log4j configuration that enables or disables  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         JNDI lookups or remote resource fetches.                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mBoolean.parseBoolean[0m[1m([0m[1;35mSystem.getProperty[0m[1m([0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndi"[0m, [32m"false"[0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;`            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - **Result of patch**                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           On recompilation, Maven fails with                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m             `cannot assign a value to final variable ENABLE_JNDI`                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m           indicating that elsewhere in `JndiLookup.java` there is still an assignment to    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ENABLE_JNDI`, which is now declared `final`.                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ---                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Description                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m. **Initial issue details**                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - A Jazzer sanitizer [1m([0m`NamingContextLookup.lookupHook`[1m)[0m intercepted a JNDI       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         lookup in `org.apache.logging.log4j.core.lookup.JndiLookup.lookup`.                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The fuzzed input led Log4j’s substitution logic [1m([0m`StrSubstitutor`,             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `PatternLayout`[1m)[0m to invoke JNDI against a remote URL.                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Depending on the JDK, this can result in remote code execution or leaking      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         sensitive data from the JVM.                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m. **Key observations from the initial report**                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The vulnerability arises because `ENABLE_JNDI` was unconditionally `true`.     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The JNDI plugin is wired into the lookup and formatting pipeline, so any       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         logged string containing a `$[1m{[0mjndi:[33m...[0m[1m}[0m` expression triggers the lookup.            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m. **Patch attempt details**                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - File modified:                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Original lines [1m([0mapproximate[1m)[0m:                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              private static boolean ENABLE_JNDI = true;                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [33m...[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              [35m/[0m[35m/[0m later in the class:                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ENABLE_JNDI = [1;35msomeCondition[0m[1m([0m[1m)[0m;  [35m/[0m[35m/[0m line ~[1;36m82[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Patched lines:                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              private static final boolean ENABLE_JNDI =                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                  [1;35mBoolean.parseBoolean[0m[1m([0m[1;35mSystem.getProperty[0m[1m([0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndi"[0m, [32m"false"[0m[1m)[0m[1m)[0m;    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              ```                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - The intent was to disable JNDI lookups by default and allow enabling via       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `-Dlog4j2.[33menableJndi[0m=[35mtrue[0m`.                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m. **Compilation failure after patch**                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - Error message:                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              `[35m/[0m[95mJndiLookup.java[0m:[1m[[0m[1;36m82[0m,[1;36m9[0m[1m][0m cannot assign a value to final variable ENABLE_JNDI`  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - This indicates that the code at line [1;36m82[0m still performs an assignment to        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ENABLE_JNDI`, which now contradicts its `final` declaration.                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m. **Areas for further investigation**                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - **JndiLookup.java**                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – The block around line [1;36m82[0m where `ENABLE_JNDI` is reassigned. Remove or        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         refactor that assignment.                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – Any static initializer or methods that toggle `ENABLE_JNDI`.                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - **Lookup registration and configuration**                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – How the `jndi` plugin is registered in `PluginManager` or `plugin.xml`.      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – Any other code paths that refer to `ENABLE_JNDI`.                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m            - **Test suite and benchmarks**                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – Unit tests or integration tests that assume the default behavior of          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `ENABLE_JNDI`.                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m              – Fuzzer harnesses that may need updating to reflect the new property.         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         This evaluation captures the observed vulnerability, the attempted mitigation via a [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         system property, and the compilation conflict introduced by making the flag         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         `final`. Further code review should focus on reconciling the `final` declaration    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         with existing assignments and ensuring consistent configuration of JNDI lookups.    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ## Initial Issue Log                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         Here is the initial issue log of the codebase:                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1m<[0m[1;95missue[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     private static final boolean ENABLE_JNDI =[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;35mBoolean.parseBoolean[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mSystem.getProperty[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndi"[0m[39m, [0m[32m"false"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Remove the mutable setter method [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`public static void [0m[1;35msetEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentirely [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m81[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m83[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. No other code or tests invoke it, and runtime toggling is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot required once JNDI is controlled by a system property.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve the public read-only API:[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep `public static boolean [0m[1;35misEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` so external consumers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand tests[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcan check the flag.[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Verify the lookup logic remains unchanged:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The null check and `!ENABLE_JNDI` guard [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m54[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m56[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m stay intact, ensuring [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookups short-circuit when disabled.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Ensure tests continue to pass:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `JndiLookupTest` uses `if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mJndiLookup.isEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return;` at the top of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits `@Test` method. With the default system property `[0m[32m"false"[0m[39m`, the test will skip [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mits assertions, which is acceptable behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mJUnit treats an early return as a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpassed test[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. No changes to test code are necessary.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Documentation update [0m[1;39m([0m[39moptional but recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In the class-level Javadoc or `log4j2.properties` reference, note that JNDI [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookups are disabled by default and can be enabled via `-Dlog4j2.[0m[33menableJndi[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m`.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Validate:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Recompile with Maven to confirm the removal of the compilation error.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the full test suite to verify no regressions.[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Execute a Jazzer fuzzing session to confirm that `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:[0m[33m...[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` no longer [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mperforms lookups unless explicitly enabled by the system property.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Removing the setter eliminates the illegal assignment to a `final` field while [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserving the new, secure default of JNDI lookups being disabled.[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The existing lookup logic and public getter remain unchanged, ensuring no [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdownstream functionality is broken.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tests are unaffected, because they already guard on `[0m[1;35misEnableJndi[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. Skipping [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe test when JNDI is disabled is consistent with the new security posture.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This approach localizes the fix to `JndiLookup.java`, avoids modifying harness or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtest code, and implements the intended system-property configuration pattern [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout unintended side effects.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
